    <script>
        function getCookie(name) {
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
        }
    </script>
    <script>
        (function () {
            // check if sat_track cookie exists
            var check = getCookie('sat_track');

            if (check === undefined) {
                // list of geos where only strictly necessary cookies are allowed
                let SNGeos = ["GB", "BE"];
                if (SNGeos.indexOf(window.otUserLocation) !== -1) {
                    document.cookie = "sat_track=false;path=/;secure;max-age=31536000";
                }
                else {
                    document.cookie = "sat_track=true;path=/;secure;max-age=31536000";
                }
                console.log("creating sat_track");
            }
        }());
    </script>

/*
 * version='1.0' 
 * OneTrustCookieHelper
 * contains helper classes for OneTrust Cookie Consent Management
 * this will help in cookie detection and blocking
 */
(function (root, factory) {  
    /*
    * Browser globals
    */
    root.OneTrustCookieHelper = factory();
    root.OneTrustCookieHelper.init(root.OnetrustActiveGroups);
 
}(typeof self !== 'undefined' ? self : this,
  function () {
    var ACTIVE_GROUPS_ID = [1, 2, 3, 4];
    var activeCookieCategories = {
      StrictlyNecessary: false,
      FirstPartyAnalytics: false,
      PeformanceFunctional: false,
      SocialMediaAdvertising: false
    };

    /*
     * setActiveGroups - sets activeCookieCategories object (active cookie groups) 
     * based on global variable OnetrustActiveGroups
     * parameters: 
     * OneTrustActiveGroups - global variable created by OneTrust script
     */
    var setActiveGroups = function (OnetrustActiveGroups) {
      // exit function if OneTrustActiveGroups data is invalid
      if (!(OnetrustActiveGroups &amp;&amp; OnetrustActiveGroups.length &gt; 0)) {
        return false;
      }
      // reset active groups
      this.resetActiveGroups();
      // proceed with active category checking
      var that = this;
      ACTIVE_GROUPS_ID.forEach(function (currId) {
        var regex = new RegExp(',' + currId + ',', 'g');
        // check if current id is active
        if ((regex.exec(OnetrustActiveGroups)) !== null) {
          // set active group to true
          switch (currId) {
            case 1:
              that.activeCookieCategories.StrictlyNecessary = true;
              break;
            case 2:
              that.activeCookieCategories.FirstPartyAnalytics = true;
              break;
            case 3:
              that.activeCookieCategories.PeformanceFunctional = true;
              break;
            case 4:
              that.activeCookieCategories.SocialMediaAdvertising = true;
              break;
            default:
              break;
          }
        }
      });
    };

    /*
     * reset activeCookieCategories to false
     */
    var resetActiveGroups = function () {
      this.activeCookieCategories = {
        StrictlyNecessary: false,
        FirstPartyAnalytics: false,
        PeformanceFunctional: false,
        SocialMediaAdvertising: false
      };
    }
    /*
     * resetCookie - expire cookies for it to be reset
     * only affects EU users if the date of interaction to the cookie banner happened before set date in OnetrustCookieClosedDate
     */
	var resetCookie = function () {
            userLocation = window.otUserLocation;
            //exit function if userLocation is undefined
            if (typeof userLocation === "undefined") {
                return;
            }

            if (_satellite.getVar("OneTrust_SNGeoList").indexOf(userLocation) &gt; -1 || _satellite.getVar("OneTrust_EUGeoList").indexOf(userLocation) &gt; -1) {
                var cookieClosed = getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed');
                //check if OptanonAlerBoxClosed exists
                if (cookieClosed !== undefined) {
                    var closeDate = cookieClosed.slice(0, 10);
                    //expire cookies for it to be reset if closeDate is before OnetrustCookieClosedDate
                    if (closeDate &lt; _satellite.getVar("OneTrustCookieClosedDate")) {
                        if (_satellite.getVar("site_domain") == "www.accenture.com") {
                            document.cookie = "OptanonAlertBoxClosed=; expires=Wed, 08 July 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/; domain=.accenture.com;";
                            document.cookie = "OptanonConsent=; expires=Wed, 08 July 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/; domain=.accenture.com;";
                        }
                        else {
                            document.cookie = "OptanonAlertBoxClosed=; expires=Wed, 08 July 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;";
                            document.cookie = "OptanonConsent=; expires=Wed, 08 July 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;";
                        }
                        //set default cookie settings based on the userLocation 
                        if (_satellite.getVar("OneTrust_SNGeoList").indexOf(userLocation) &gt; -1) {
                            window.OptanonActiveGroups = ",1,";
                        }
                        else {
                            window.OptanonActiveGroups = ",1,2,";
                        }
                        _satellite.logger.log(closeDate + " - onetrust cookies deleted");
                    }
                    else {
                        _satellite.logger.log(closeDate + " - onetrust cookies retained");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    _satellite.logger.log("no OptanonAlertBoxClosed");
                }
            }
            else {
                _satellite.logger.log(userLocation + " - no action");
            }
        }
    
    /*
     * init - initialize method for OneTrustCookieHelper module
     * calls methods setActiveGroups,  
     */
    var init = function (OnetrustActiveGroups) {
      this.setActiveGroups(OnetrustActiveGroups);
      this.resetCookie();
    };

    return {
      // properties
      activeCookieCategories: activeCookieCategories,
      // methods
      init: init,
      setActiveGroups: setActiveGroups,
      resetActiveGroups: resetActiveGroups,
      resetCookie : resetCookie
    };
  }));

function addObjectKeysPolyfill(){
    if (!Object.keys) {
        Object.keys = (function() {
            'use strict';
            var hasOwnProperty = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty,
                hasDontEnumBug = !({ toString: null }).propertyIsEnumerable('toString'),
                dontEnums = [
                'toString',
                'toLocaleString',
                'valueOf',
                'hasOwnProperty',
                'isPrototypeOf',
                'propertyIsEnumerable',
                'constructor'
                ],
                dontEnumsLength = dontEnums.length;

            return function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj !== 'function' &amp;&amp; (typeof obj !== 'object' || obj === null)) {
                throw new TypeError('Object.keys called on non-object');
            }

            var result = [], prop, i;

            for (prop in obj) {
                if (hasOwnProperty.call(obj, prop)) {
                result.push(prop);
                }
            }

            if (hasDontEnumBug) {
                for (i = 0; i &lt; dontEnumsLength; i++) {
                if (hasOwnProperty.call(obj, dontEnums[i])) {
                    result.push(dontEnums[i]);
                }
                }
            }
            return result;
            };
        }());
    }
}

function getDemandbaseParameters(profile, trgAttrs){
  var dmdBaseParams = {};
    
  for(var i=0;i&lt;trgAttrs.length;i++){
    if(profile.hasOwnProperty(trgAttrs[i])){
      dmdBaseParams["profile."+ trgAttrs[i]] = encodeURIComponent(profile[trgAttrs[i]]);
    }
  }
    
  window.targetPageParams = function(){
    return dmdBaseParams;
  }
}

function sendGlobalMbox(){
  document.documentElement.style.opacity = "0";
  adobe.target.getOffer({
    "mbox": "target-global-mbox",
    "success": function(offers) {
        adobe.target.applyOffer({
        "mbox": "target-global-mbox",
        "offer": offers
      });
      document.documentElement.style.opacity = "1";
    },
    "error": function(status, error) {
      if (console &amp;&amp; console.log) {
        console.log(status);
        console.log(error);
      }
      document.documentElement.style.opacity = "1";
    },
    "timeout": 5000
  });
}

function poll() {
    pollCount++;

    var profile = {};

    if (window.Dmdbase_CDC) { 
      if(window.Dmdbase_CDC.CompanyProfile &amp;&amp; typeof window.Dmdbase_CDC.CompanyProfile === "object"){
        profile = window.Dmdbase_CDC.CompanyProfile;
      }
        
      getDemandbaseParameters(profile, window.Dmdbase_CDC.targetAttributes);
    }

    if(typeof window.targetPageParams === "function" &amp;&amp; Object.keys(window.targetPageParams()).length &gt; 0){
      window.targetPageParams();
      sendGlobalMbox();
      clearTimeout(poll);
    }
    else if(pollCount === MAX_POLL_COUNT){
      sendGlobalMbox();
      clearTimeout(poll);
    }
    else if(pollCount &lt; MAX_POLL_COUNT) {
      setTimeout(poll, POLL_INTERVAL);
    }
}

try {
  var POLL_INTERVAL = 10;

  // Max number of poll attempts
  var MAX_POLL_COUNT = 10;

  var pollCount = 0;

  addObjectKeysPolyfill();
  poll();

} catch (e) {
  console.log(e);
  document.documentElement.style.opacity = "1";
}

window.acnLimelight = {
    trackPause: false,

    timeTriggered: "",
    mediaSegment: "",
    isVideoPaused: false,
    ContinuePauseTracking: true,
    Cache: {
        SkipPauseTrackingKey: "lvp_skippausetracking",
        AutoPlayExecuted: "mpm_autoplayexecuted",
        AutoPlay: "mpm_autoplay",
        AutoPause: "mpm_autopause"
    },
    Events: {
        PlayStateChanged: "onPlayStateChanged"
    },
    limelightPlayerCallback: function (playerId, eventName, data) {
        if (playerId !== "limelight_player_453141") {
            switch (eventName) {
                case 'onPlayerLoad':
                    LimelightPlayer.registerPlayer(playerId);
                    acnLimelight.doOnLimelightPlayerLoad(playerId);
                    break;
                case 'onMediaLoad':
                    acnLimelight.doOnLimelightPlayerLoad(playerId);
                    acnLimelight.doOnDelveMediaLoad(data, playerId);
                    break;
                case 'onMediaComplete':
                    acnLimelight.doOnDelveMediaComplete(data, playerId);
                    break;
                case 'onPlayheadUpdate':
                    acnLimelight.doOnDelvePlayheadUpdate(data, playerId);
                    break;
                case 'onPlayStateChanged':
                    acnLimelight.doOnDelvePlayheadUpdate(data, playerId, acnLimelight.Events.PlayStateChanged);
                    break;
            }
        }
        if (typeof customLimelightPlayerCallback === 'function') {
            window.customLimelightPlayerCallback(playerId, eventName, data);
        }
    },
    doOnLimelightPlayerLoad: function (playerId) {
        acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId] = {
            playInitiatedForMedia: false,
            completeInitiatedForMedia: false,
            timePositionSeconds: 0
        };
    },
    doOnDelveMediaLoad: function (e, playerId) {
        var mTitle = "";
        var videoIDValue = jQuery("#" + playerId)[0];
        if (typeof videoIDValue === 'undefined') {
            videoIDValue = jQuery("[name='" + playerId + "']")[0];
        }
        var videoCurrentMedia;
        if (typeof videoIDValue === 'undefined') {
            videoCurrentMedia = videoIDValue.doGetCurrentMedia();
        }
        var documentPlayerMedia = document[playerId];
        if (typeof this[playerId] !== 'undefined') {
            mTitle = this[playerId].doGetCurrentMedia().title + ".mp4";
        } else if (typeof LimelightPlayer[playerId] !== 'undefined') {
            mTitle = LimelightPlayer[playerId].doGetCurrentMedia().title + ".mp4";
        } else if (documentPlayerMedia &amp;&amp; typeof documentPlayerMedia !== "function" &amp;&amp; typeof documentPlayerMedia.doGetCurrentMedia === "function") {
            mTitle = documentPlayerMedia.doGetCurrentMedia().title + ".mp4";
        } else if (typeof videoIDValue !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; videoIDValue.id === playerId &amp;&amp; typeof videoCurrentMedia !== 'undefined') {
            mTitle = videoCurrentMedia.title + ".mp4";
        } else {
            if (e.title) {
                mTitle = e.title + ".mp4";
            } else {
                mTitle = playerId;
            }
        }
        if (acnLimelight.isMobileOverrideMediaTitle(LimelightPlayer[playerId], mTitle, playerId))
            mTitle = e.title + ".mp4";

        mTitle = mTitle &amp;&amp; mTitle.length ? mTitle.toLowerCase().trim() : "";
        var videoLengthInSeconds = Math.floor(e.durationInMilliseconds / 1000);

        acnLimelight.media[playerId] = {
            mediaTitle: mTitle,
            durationInSeconds: videoLengthInSeconds,
            durationInMilliseconds: e.durationInMilliseconds

        };
    },
    doOnDelvePlayheadUpdate: function (e, playerId, playerEvent) {
        var deltaSeconds;
        var playerTimePositionInSeconds = acnLimelight.getPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId);
        if (typeof (e.isBusy) === 'undefined' &amp;&amp; (isMobile() || isTablet() || IsTouch())) {
            e.isBusy = false;
        }

        if (e.positionInMilliseconds) {
            acnLimelight.setPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId, e.positionInMilliseconds);
            acnLimelight.durationSeconds = e.durationInMilliseconds / 1000;
            playerTimePositionInSeconds = acnLimelight.getPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId);
            deltaSeconds = e.durationInMilliseconds / 1000 - playerTimePositionInSeconds;
            acnLimelight.trackMileStone(e.positionInMilliseconds, playerId);
        }


        if (acnLimelight.isTrackVideoPauseEvent(e, playerId, deltaSeconds, playerEvent)) {
            acnLimelight.trackPause = true;
            acnLimelight.trackLimelightPlayer("pause", playerId, playerTimePositionInSeconds, e);
            acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].playInitiatedForMedia = false;
            acnLimelight.isVideoPaused = true;
        } else if (playerTimePositionInSeconds &gt;= 1) {
            if (e.isPlaying === true &amp;&amp; e.isBusy === false &amp;&amp; acnLimelight.isVideoPaused == false) {
                acnLimelight.setPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId, 0);
                playerTimePositionInSeconds = 0;
            }

            if (!acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].playInitiatedForMedia) {
                acnLimelight.setPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId, e.positionInMilliseconds);
                playerTimePositionInSeconds = acnLimelight.getPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId);

                if (Math.floor(playerTimePositionInSeconds) != 0) {
                    acnLimelight.trackLimelightPlayer("start", playerId, playerTimePositionInSeconds, e);
                    acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].playInitiatedForMedia = true;
                }
            }
        } else if (e.isPlaying &amp;&amp; e.isBusy === false &amp;&amp; !acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].playInitiatedForMedia) {
            acnLimelight.trackLimelightPlayer("start", playerId, playerTimePositionInSeconds, e);
            acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].playInitiatedForMedia = true;
        }


    },

    doOnDelveMediaComplete: function (e, playerId) {
        var lmPlayer = acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId];
        if (!(lmPlayer &amp;&amp; lmPlayer.completeInitiatedForMedia)) {
            lmPlayer.completeInitiatedForMedia = true;
            acnLimelight.trackLimelightPlayer("complete", playerId, e.durationInMilliseconds / 1000);
            acnLimelight.trackPause = false;
        }
    },
    trackLimelightPlayer: function (milestone, playerId, timePosition, e) {
        acnLimelight.triggeredPlayer = playerId;

        if (!isNaN(timePosition)) {
            acnLimelight.timeTriggered = Math.floor(timePosition).toString();
        } else {
            acnLimelight.timeTriggered = Math.floor(acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].timePositionSeconds).toString();
        }

        acnLimelight.setCurrentMediaFieldValues(playerId);
      
        var videoNotStarted = acnLimelight.isVideoNotStarted(playerId);
      
        switch (milestone) {
            case 'start':

                if ((acnLimelight.timeTriggered === "1" || "0") &amp;&amp; videoNotStarted) {
                    
                    acnLimelight.mediaSegment = "1:M:0-25";
                    _satellite.track("DCR_Limelight_Video_Start");
                  
                    acnLimelight.media[playerId].videoStarted = true;
                    
                   _satellite.logger.log("Limelight Video Player &gt; " + playerId + " starts playing."); 
                  
                }

                break;
            case 'pause':
                _satellite.logger.log("Limelight Video Player &gt; " + playerId + " is on pause state.");                
                break;
            case 'complete':
                acnLimelight.mediaSegment = "2:M:75-100";
                _satellite.track("DCR_Limelight_Video_Complete");
                _satellite.logger.log("Limelight Video Player &gt; " + playerId + " playing is completed.");
              
                break;
        }
    },
    isTrackVideoPauseEvent: function (e, playerId, deltaSeconds, playerEvent) {
        var isTrackPauseEvent = true;
        var playerTimePositionInSeconds = acnLimelight.getPlayerTimePositionInSeconds(playerId);

        if (playerEvent === acnLimelight.Events.PlayStateChanged) {
            var skipPauseTracking = acncm.CacheManager.read(acnLimelight.Cache.SkipPauseTrackingKey);
            if (skipPauseTracking) {
                acncm.CacheManager.remove(acnLimelight.Cache.SkipPauseTrackingKey);
                acnLimelight.ContinuePauseTracking = false;
            }
        }

        //Not in Pause State Conditions
        if (e.isPlaying !== false)
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;

        if (e.isBusy !== false)
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;

        if (typeof deltaSeconds !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; deltaSeconds &lt; 1)
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;

        if ((acnLimelight.durationSeconds - playerTimePositionInSeconds) &lt; 1)
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;

        if (acnLimelight.ContinuePauseTracking === false) {
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;
            acnLimelight.ContinuePauseTracking = true;
        }
        if (acnLimelight.trackPause == false || playerTimePositionInSeconds === 0) {
            isTrackPauseEvent = false;
            acnLimelight.trackPause = true;
        }

        //Pause State Condition
        if (e.isPlaying === false &amp;&amp; typeof e.isBusy === "undefined")
            isTrackPauseEvent = true;

        return isTrackPauseEvent;
    },

    skipPauseTrackingOnVideoOverlayClosed: function (elm) {
        var $overlayCloseButton = jQuery(elm);
        var isValidElem = $overlayCloseButton.hasClass("popupvid-x-button");
        var hasExpectedParent = $overlayCloseButton.closest("p.popupvid-x-button-container").length &gt; 0;
        if (isValidElem &amp;&amp; hasExpectedParent) {
            acncm.CacheManager.write(acnLimelight.Cache.SkipPauseTrackingKey, 1);
        }
    },
    isMobileOverrideMediaTitle: function (limeLightPlayer, mediaTitle, playerId) {
        if (isMobile() == false)
            return false;
        if (typeof limeLightPlayer !== "undefined")
            return false;
        if (mediaTitle === playerId)
            return true;
    },

    isVideoObject: function (tagName) {
        var clickedIsVideo = false;
        if (tagName.indexOf("VIDEO") &gt; -1) {
            clickedIsVideo = true;
        }
        return clickedIsVideo;
    },

    isMediaPlayerDoesNotExists: function (playerId) {

        if (typeof acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId] === "undefined")
            return true;

        return false;
    },

    setPlayerTimePositionInSeconds: function (playerId, timePositionInMilliseconds) {

        if (acnLimelight.isMediaPlayerDoesNotExists(playerId))
            return;

        acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].timePositionSeconds = timePositionInMilliseconds / 1000;

    },

    getPlayerTimePositionInSeconds: function (playerId) {

        if (acnLimelight.isMediaPlayerDoesNotExists(playerId))
            return 0;

        return acnLimelight.mediaPlayers[playerId].timePositionSeconds;
    },

    trackMileStone: function (timePosition, playerId) {
        if (timePosition &lt; 1)
            return;


        var mediaDuration = acnLimelight.media[playerId].durationInMilliseconds;
        var mediaDurationInSeconds = acnLimelight.media[playerId].durationInSeconds;
        var timePostionInSeconds = Math.floor(timePosition / 1000);

        //Exit and remove tracking related data on video complete.
        if (mediaDurationInSeconds === timePostionInSeconds) {
            acnLimelight.clearVideoTrackingData(playerId);
            return;
        }

        var m25 = Math.floor((mediaDuration * 0.25) / 1000);
        var m50 = Math.floor((mediaDuration * 0.50) / 1000);
        var m75 = Math.floor((mediaDuration * 0.75) / 1000);



        var isMP25NotExist = typeof acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp25 === "undefined" ? true : false;
        var isMP50NotExist = typeof acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp50 === "undefined" ? true : false;
        var isMP75NotExist = typeof acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp75 === "undefined" ? true : false;

        var mileStonePercentage = 0;

        if (m25 &lt;= timePostionInSeconds &amp;&amp; isMP25NotExist) {

            acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp25 = timePostionInSeconds;
            mileStonePercentage = 25;

        } else if (m50 &lt;= timePostionInSeconds &amp;&amp; isMP50NotExist) {

            acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp50 = timePostionInSeconds;
            mileStonePercentage = 50;

        } else if (m75 &lt;= timePostionInSeconds &amp;&amp; isMP75NotExist) {
                        
            acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp75 = timePostionInSeconds;
            mileStonePercentage = 75;
        }

        if (mileStonePercentage) {
            acnLimelight.setCurrentMediaFieldValues(playerId);
            _satellite.setVar("limelightPlayer_milestonePercentage", mileStonePercentage);
            _satellite.track("DCR_Limelight_Video_Milestone");
            _satellite.logger.log("Limelight Player Video MileStone "+ mileStonePercentage +"%: " + timePosition);
        }

    },

    setCurrentMediaFieldValues: function (playerId) {

        var currentMedia = acnLimelight.media[playerId];

        _satellite.setVar("limelightPlayer_videoId", playerId.toLowerCase());
        _satellite.setVar("limelightPlayer_videoTitle", currentMedia.mediaTitle.toLowerCase());
        _satellite.setVar("limelightPlayer_videoDuration", currentMedia.durationInSeconds);
    },
      
    isVideoNotStarted: function (playerId) {

        if (typeof acnLimelight.media[playerId].videoStarted === "undefined")
            return true;

        return false;
    },

    clearVideoTrackingData: function (playerId) {

        if (acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp25)
            delete acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp25;

        if (acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp50)
            delete acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp50;

        if (acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp75)
            delete acnLimelight.media[playerId].mp75;

        if (acnLimelight.media[playerId].videoStarted)
            delete acnLimelight.media[playerId].videoStarted
    }

};

function limelightPlayerCallback(playerId, eventName, data) {    
      window.acnLimelight.limelightPlayerCallback(playerId, eventName, data);
}
</script><script>
var JobSearchPrefiltered = {
	queryStrings : ["jk", "jt", "ct", "sk", "ba", "sp", "tl"],
	searchFilterList: [],
	qryParamValList:[],

	IsQueryStringExists: function (pageURL) {
		//reset list
		this.searchFilterList = [];
		this.qryParamValList = adobe_s.getQueryStringParameters(pageURL);

		for (var indx = 0; indx &lt; this.qryParamValList.length; indx++) {
		var qryParam = this.qryParamValList[indx];
		if (jQuery.inArray(qryParam.key, this.queryStrings) &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; this.qryParamValList[indx].value)
		return true;
		}

		return false;

	},
	
	GetSearchFilters: function (pageURL) {
        function GetPrefix(queryString,qryParamValue) {
        	function insertPrefix(prefix,arrQryParamValue) {
        		for (var i=0; i &lt; arrQryParamValue.length; i++ ) {
        			if (prefix === "travel:") {
                         arrQryParamValue[i] = prefix + arrQryParamValue[i] + "%";
                     }
                     else {
                         arrQryParamValue[i] = prefix + arrQryParamValue[i];
                     }
        		}
        		qryParamValue = arrQryParamValue.join('|');
        		return qryParamValue;
        	}
        	if (qryParamValue) {
        		qryParamValue = qryParamValue.split('|');
                if (queryString === "jt") {
					return insertPrefix("job type:",qryParamValue);
				} else if (queryString === "ct") {
					return insertPrefix("city:",qryParamValue);
				} else if (queryString === "sk") {
					return insertPrefix("skill:",qryParamValue);
				} else if (queryString === "sp") {
					return insertPrefix("specialization:",qryParamValue);
				} else if (queryString === "ba") {
					return insertPrefix("business area:",qryParamValue);
				} else if (queryString === "tl") {
					return insertPrefix("travel:",qryParamValue);
				} else {
					return "";
				}
        	}
		}
		var numberOfFilters = this.qryParamValList.length;
		if (numberOfFilters === 0)
		return "";

		for(var indx = (adobe_s.Util.getQueryParam("jk") ? 1 : 0); indx &lt; this.queryStrings.length; indx++) {
        var queryString = this.queryStrings[indx];
		var qryParamValue = adobe_s.Util.getQueryParam(queryString,pageURL); 
			if(qryParamValue.length){
				this.searchFilterList.push(GetPrefix(queryString,qryParamValue));
				numberOfFilters--;
			}
			//exit iteration if all query strings are pushed to the array.
			if(numberOfFilters === 0)
			break;
		}
		if(this.searchFilterList.length === 1)
		return this.searchFilterList[0];

		return this.searchFilterList.join('|');
	}
}

</script><script>
var ProductStringBuilder = {
    EventsArr: [],
    SetProductString: function (evarsToInclude) {
        var eVarsArr = []; //local variable for preparing the eVars string
        var contString = [];
        var category = "";
        var moduleName = _satellite.getVar("moduleName");
        var contentId = moduleName ? moduleName.replace(/\;/g, "") : "";
        var qty = "";
        var price = "";

        for (var key in evarsToInclude) {
            if (evarsToInclude.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                var eVarContent = _satellite.getVar(evarsToInclude[key]);
                if (typeof eVarContent === "string" &amp;&amp; eVarContent.length &gt; 0) {
                    eVarsArr.push(key + "=" + eVarContent.replace(/[\;\/]/g, ""));
                    if (key === "eVar19") {
                        adobe_s.list3 = eVarContent;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        contString.push(category);
        contString.push(contentId);
        contString.push(qty);
        contString.push(price);
        contString.push(ProductStringBuilder.EventsArr.join("|"));
        contString.push(eVarsArr.join("|"));
        // Compile product string
        adobe_s.products = contString.join(";");
        ProductStringBuilder.EventsArr = []; //reset eventsArr
    },
  
    AddEventToAdobe: function(eventName, obj, addToProductString) {
        if (addToProductString) {
            ProductStringBuilder.EventsArr.push(eventName + '=1');
        }
        obj.events = adobe_s.apl(obj.events, eventName, ',', 1);
        obj.linkTrackEvents = adobe_s.apl(obj.linkTrackEvents, eventName, ',', 1);
    }
}

(function (root, factory) {

    VidyardPlugin.init();

})(typeof self !== "undefined" ? self : this, function (jQuery) {

    var init = function () {
        function startVideoTracking(player, chapter, percentProgress) {
            // send data to an analytics backend
            _satellite.setVar("vidyardTitle", player.metadata.chapters_attributes[chapter].video_attributes.name.toLowerCase());
            _satellite.setVar("vidyardDuration", player.metadata.chapters_attributes[chapter].video_attributes.length_in_seconds);
            _satellite.setVar("vidyardVideoId", player.uuid.toLowerCase());
            var $this = jQuery(player.element);

            varsToRemove.forEach(function (e) {
                adobe_s.linkTrackVars = adobe_s.linkTrackVars.replace(e, "");
            });

            switch (percentProgress) {
                case 1: _satellite.track("vidyardVideo_Start", {"element": $this}); break;
                case 25: _satellite.track("vidyardVideo_25", {"element": $this}); break;
                case 50: _satellite.track("vidyardVideo_50", {"element": $this}); break;
                case 75: _satellite.track("vidyardVideo_75", {"element": $this}); break;
                case 100: _satellite.track("vidyardVideo_Complete", {"element": $this}); break;
            }
        }

        function registerProgressEvents(vidyardEmbed) {
            vidyardEmbed.api.progressEvents(function (result) {
                startVideoTracking(result.player, result.chapter, result.event);
            }, [1, 25, 50, 75, 100]);
        }

        var varsToRemove = [
            "eVar69,",
            "eVar70,",
            "eVar45,",
            "eVar46,",
            "prop6,",
            "prop45,"
        ];

        if (window.vidyardEmbed) {
            registerProgressEvents(window.vidyardEmbed);
        }
        else {
            window.onVidyardAPI = function (vidyardEmbed) {
                registerProgressEvents(vidyardEmbed);
            }
        }
    }

    return {
        init: init,
    };

});

/*
 * waitForDataModel
 * Used to make page view wait for dataModel is ready
 *
 * Rules that call waitForDataModel:
 * "Listener - All Pages - Listen for DataModel"
 */
// Amazingly, Launch allows this "Listener - All Pages - Listen for Data Model" rule to fire prior to running the Adobe Analytics extension code, so adobe_s is undefined here.
// So we have to create this function here, outside of the adobe_s namespace.
function isDataModelReady() {
  //Wait for blogs
  if (document.location.href.indexOf("/blogs/") &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; dataModel.page.pageInfo.blogs) {
      return true;
  }
  //Wait for user
  if (dataModel.user) {
      return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

function isDataJobCountReady() {
  //Wait for data-job-count
  if (document.location.href.indexOf("/careers/jobsearch")  &gt; -1) {
    var dataJobCount = jQuery('a#latest-nav').attr('data-job-count');
    if (dataJobCount != undefined) { 
      return true;
    }
    else {
      return false;
    }
  }
  else {
    return true;
  }
}

var timesWaited = 0;
function waitForDataModel(functionToFire, param1, param2){
  if (typeof dataModel != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; isDataModelReady() &amp;&amp; typeof adobe_s != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; isDataJobCountReady()){
    if (timesWaited &gt; 0){
      _satellite.logger.log("&gt;&gt;&gt; waitForDataModel: Waited for dataModel &amp; adobe_s : ..." + timesWaited / 10 + " seconds. Firing page view call...");
    }
    else{
      _satellite.logger.log("&gt;&gt;&gt; waitForDataModel: dataModel &amp; adobe_s already available. Firing page view call...");
    }
    timesWaited = 0;
    if (typeof digitalData !== "undefined") {
      adobe_s.PageMetadata.collectPageMetadata();
    }
    functionToFire(param1, param2);
  }
  else {
    timesWaited++;
    setTimeout(waitForDataModel, 100, functionToFire, param1, param2);
  }
}


// Set isPageViewFiring here on a temporary object because this may be running prior to the Adobe Analytics extension code running.
// isPageViewFiring gets set to false in the callback function defined in the Adobe Analytics extension
window.adobeTemp = window.adobeTemp ? window.adobeTemp : {};
window.adobeTemp.isPageViewFiring = true;

// Call "DCR - Page View" when dataModel is finally defined
waitForDataModel(_satellite.track, 'dataModelReady');
});</script><script>
